1a1(mngon pa): @##/
1b1(mngon pa): /rgya gar skad du/ lo ka pradz+nyA/ bod skad du/ 'jig rten gzhag pa/ bam po dang po/ bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /de nas/ stong rnams dang ni rol
1b2(mngon pa): mtsho dang / /ngan song gsum dang gling dang shing / /dga' tshal dang ni mkha' lding dang / /rgyal chen grong dang 'dus pa rnams/ /'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan
1b3(mngon pa): 'das mnyan yod na rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal mgon med zas sbyin gyi kun dga' ra ba na bzhugs te/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis dge slong rnams la bka' stsal pa/ dge slong dag 'jig rten
1b4(mngon pa): gyi khams ni gsum po 'di dag yin te/ gang dag yin zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ stong chung ngu'i 'jig rten gyi khams dang / stong gnyis pa bar ma'i 'jig rten gyi khams dang / stong gsum gyi
1b5(mngon pa): stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams so/ /stong chung ngu'i 'jig rten gyi khams gang zhe na/ stong gsum gyi 'jig rten gyi khams na nyi ma rnam par snang ba rnams kun du 'khor zhing phyogs snang bar
2a1(mngon pa): byed pa ci yod pa de nyid kyi yin te/ zla ba stong dang / nyi ma stong dang / ri'i rgyal po ri rab stong dang / shar gyi lus 'phags po stong dang / /lho'i 'dzam bu'i gling stong dang / /nub kyi ba lang spyod stong dang / /byang
2a2(mngon pa): gi sgra mi snyan stong dang / /rgyal chen bzhi pa'i lha'i ris stong dang / /sum cu rtsa gsum pa stong dang / /'thab bral ba stong dang / dga' ldan pa stong dang / 'phrul dga' ba stong dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa stong dang / tshangs
2a3(mngon pa): pa'i 'jig rten stong ste/ dge slong dag 'di ni stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams zhes bya'o/ /stong gnyis pa bar ma'i 'jig rten gyi khams gang zhe na/ stong chung ngu'i 'jig rten gyi khams stong gang yin pa de ni stong gnyis pa bar
2a4(mngon pa): ma'i 'jig rten gyi khams zhes bya'o/ /stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i khams gang zhe na/ dge slong dag stong gnyis pa bar ma'i 'jig rten gyi khams stong gang yin pa de ni stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams zhes bya'o/ /
2a5(mngon pa): dge slong dag de lta bu'i stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams rnams shar phyogs su mtha' med cing mu med la/ 'jig pa'am/ zhig par gnas shing / chags pa'am chags par gnas te/ gzhan 'jig cing
2b1(mngon pa): gzhan zhig par gnas la/ gzhan chags shing gzhan 'chags par gnas so/ /dge slong dag 'di lta bur stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams lho dang / nub dang / byang gi phyogs su mtha' med cing mu med la/ 'jig pa'am/ zhig par gnas shing / chags
2b2(mngon pa): pa'am 'chags par gnas te/ gzhan 'jig cing gzhan zhig par gnas la/ gzhan chags shing gzhan 'chags par gnas so/ /dge slong dag nam mkha' la char pa'i 'bru shing rta'i srog shing tsam 'bab ste/ chu'i rgyun rnams rab tu 'bab pa na bar chad med pa de bzhin du/
2b3(mngon pa): dge slong dag ngas lha'i mig rnam par dag pa mi las 'das pas shar phyogs su de lta bu stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams mtha' med cing mu med pa/ gzhan 'jig pa'am zhig par gnas shing / chags pa'am 'chags par gnas la/ gzhan 'jig cing gzhan
2b4(mngon pa): zhig par gnas la/ gzhan chags shing gzhan 'chags par gnas pa dang / de bzhin du lho dang / nub dang / byang phyogs su de snyed kyi stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams rnams mtha' med cing mu med la 'jig pa'am/ zhig par gnas shing / chags pa'am
2b5(mngon pa): 'chags par gnas te/ gzhan 'jig cing gzhan zhig par gnas la/ gzhan 'chags shing gzhan chags par gnas pa dag kyang mthong ngo zhes bka' stsal nas/ bcom ldan 'das nang du yang dag 'jog pa'i phyir gnas khang du gshegs so/ /de'i tshe na/ tshe dang ldan pa
2b6(mngon pa): maud gal ya na chen po 'khor de nyid kyi nang du 'dus par gyur te 'dug go/ /de nas tshe dang ldan pa maud gal ya na chen pos dge slong rnams la smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa dag ji tsam du bcom ldan 'das kyis legs par bstan pa dang / 'di ltar shing rta'i srog shing gi dpes bstan pa
2b7(mngon pa): la ni legs te ngo mtshar to/ /de la stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na ri chen po nyis stong yod de/ ri'i rgyal bo ri rab stong dang / khor yug gi ri stong rnams so/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na rgya mtsho chen po nyis stong yod de/ nang gi rgya mtsho chen po stong dang /
3a1(mngon pa): phyi rol gyi rgya mtsho chen po stong rnams so/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na ri sum stong yod de/ sems can dmyal ba stong dang / dud 'gro stong dang / yi dwags stong rnams so/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na gling chen po bzhi stong yod de/
3a2(mngon pa): shar gyi lus 'phags po stong dang / lho'i 'dzam bu gling stong dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod stong dang / byang gi sgra mi snyan stong rnams so/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na shing chen po bzhi stong yod de/ 'dzam bu'i gling pa'i shing rgya mtsho'i 'gram gyi shal ma li chen po stong dang / lha
3a3(mngon pa): ma yin gyi ris kyi tsi tra pa ta li stong dang / sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i sa brtol stong rnams so/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na klu'i rigs bzhi stong yod de/ rigs sgo nga las skye ba stong dang / mngal nas skye ba stong dang / drod gsher las skye ba stong dang / rdzus te skye ba stong
3a4(mngon pa): rnams so/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na nam mkha' lding gi rigs bzhi stong yod de/ nam mkha' lding gi rigs sgo nga las skye ba stong dang / mngal nas skye ba stong dang / drod gsher las skye ba stong dang / rdzus te skye ba stong rnams so/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi
3a5(mngon pa): khams na rgyal po chen po bzhi stong yod de/ yul 'khor srung stong dang / 'phags skyes po stong dang / mig mi bzang stong dang / rnam thos kyi bu stong rnams so/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na 'gro ba lnga stong yod de/ sems can dmyal ba'i 'gro ba stong dang / dud 'gro
3a6(mngon pa): dang / yi dags dang / lha dang mi'i 'gro ba stong rnams so/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na 'dun sa chen po nyis stong yod de/ lha'i 'dun sa chos bzangs stong dang / lha ma yin gyi 'dun sa nor bzangs zhes bya ba stong rnams so/ /'jig rten gzhag pa las tshigs
3a7(mngon pa): dang po'o/ /mdo las/ skye gnas ri dang rol mtsho dang / /de bzhin sems can dmyal brgyad gzhan/ /sems can gnas dgu rab bshad de/ /las lam bcu po de bzhin no/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na 'dod pa'i skye gnas gsum yod de/ gsum gang
3b1(mngon pa): gang zhe na/ sems can 'dod pa nye bar gnas pa dag yod de/ gang dag 'dod pa nye bar gnas pa rnams la dbang phyug gis dbang byed pa dag ste/ 'di lta ste/ mi kha cig dang / lha rnams so/ /'di ni 'dod pa'i skye gnas dang po'o/ /sems can 'dod pas sprul pa dag yod de/
3b2(mngon pa): gang dag 'dod pas sprul pa dag la dbang phyug gis dbang byed pa dag ste/ 'di lta ste/ 'phrul dga'i lha rnams so/ /'di ni 'dod pa'i skye gnas gnyis pa'o/ /sems can 'dod pa'i sprul pa gzhan dag yod de/ /gang dag 'dod pa gzhan gyis sprul pa rnams la dbang phyug
3b3(mngon pa): gis dbang byed pa dag ste/ 'di lta ste/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams so/ /'di ni 'dod pa'i skye gnas gsum pa'o/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na bde ba'i skye gnas gsum yod de/ sems can gang dag lus 'di nyid la dben pa las skyes pa'i dga' ba dang
3b4(mngon pa): bde ba las brlan par byed cing yongs su brlan par byed de/ yongs su tshim par byed cing yongs su khyab par byed pa dag yod do/ /de dag lus 'di nyid la dben pa las skyes pa'i dga' ba dang / bde bas brlan par byas shing yongs su brlan par byas te/ yongs su tshim par byas
3b5(mngon pa): shing yongs su khyab par byas nas bde bar reg pa la gnas so/ /de dag bde ba de dang / bde ba la gnas pa des tshe ring zhing yun ring por gnas te/ 'di lta ste/ tshangs ris kyi lha rnams so/ /'di ni bde ba'i skye gnas dang po'o/ /sems can gang dag lus 'di nyid la ting
3b6(mngon pa): nge 'dzin las skyes pa'i dga' ba dang / bde bas brlan par byed cing yongs su brlan par byed de yongs su tshim par byed cing yongs su khyab par byed pa dag yod do/ /de dag lus 'di nyid la ting nge 'dzin las skyes pa'i dga' ba dang / bde bas brlan par byas shing yongs su brlan par
3b7(mngon pa): byas te/ yongs su tshim par byas shing yongs su khyab par byas nas bde bar reg pa la gnas so/ /de dag bde ba de dang bde ba la gnas pa des tshe ring zhing yun ring por gnas te/ 'di lta ste/ 'od gsal gyi lha rnams so/ /'di ni bde ba'i skye gnas gnyis pa'o/ /sems can
4a1(mngon pa): gang dag lus 'di nyid la dga' ba med pa'i bde bas brlan par byed pa dang / yongs su brlan par byed de/ yongs su tshim par byed cing yongs su khyab par byed pa dag yod do/ /de dag lus 'di nyid la dga' ba med pa'i bde bas brlan par byas shing yongs su brlan
4a2(mngon pa): par byas te/ yongs su tshim par byas shing yongs su khyab par byas nas bde bar reg pa la gnas so/ /de dag bde ba de dang bde ba la gnas pa des tshe ring zhing yun ring du gnas te 'di lta ste/ dge rgyas kyi lha rnams so/ /'di ni bde ba'i skye gnas gsum pa'o/ /stong spyi phud kyi
4a3(mngon pa): 'jig rten gyi khams na gser gyi ri chen po bdun stong yod de/ ri'i rgyal po gnya' shing 'dzin stong dang / gshol mda' 'dzin stong dang / seng ldeng can stong dang / blta na sdug stong dang / rta rna ri stong dang / mu khyud 'dzin stong dang / ri'i rgyal po rnam par 'dud stong rnams so/ /stong
4a4(mngon pa): spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na rol mtsho chen po bdun stong yod de/ gnya' shing 'dzin gyi rol mtsho stong dang / gshol mda' 'dzin gyi stong dang / seng ldeng can gyi stong dang / blta na sdug gi stong dang / rta rna ri'i stong dang / mu khyud 'dzin gyi stong dang / rnam par 'dud kyi rol mtsho stong
4a5(mngon pa): rnams so/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na sems can dmyal ba chen po brgyad stong yod de/ sems can dmyal ba chen po yang sos stong dang / thig nag stong dang / bsdus gzhom stong dang / ngu 'bod stong dang / ngu 'bod chen po stong dang / tsha ba stong dang / rab tu tsha ba stong
4a6(mngon pa): dang / sems can dmyal ba mnar med pa stong rnams so/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na sems can gyi gnas dgu stong yod do/ /sems can gzugs yod pa lus tha dad cing 'du shes tha dad pa dag yod de/ 'di lta ste/ mi rnams dang / lha kha cig go/ /'di ni sems
4a7(mngon pa): can gyi gnas dang po'o/ /sems can gzugs yod pa lus tha dad cing 'du shes gcig pa dag yod de/ 'di lta ste/ tshangs ris kyi lha dang po byung ba gang yin pa de dag go/ /'di ni sems can gyi gnas gnyis pa'o/ /sems can gzugs yod pa lus gcig la 'du shes tha dad pa
4b1(mngon pa): dag yod de/ 'di lta ste/ 'od gsal gyi lha rnams so/ /'di ni sems can gyi gnas gsum pa'o/ /sems can gzugs yod pa lus gcig cing 'du shes gcig pa dag yod de/ 'di lta ste/ dge rgyas kyi lha rnams so/ /'di ni sems can gyi gnas bzhi pa'o/ /sems
4b2(mngon pa): can gzugs yod pa 'du shes med cing 'du shes dang bral ba dag yod de/ 'di lta ste/ 'du shes med pa'i lha rnams so/ /'di ni sems can gyi gnas lnga pa'o/ /sems can gzugs med pa rnam pa thams cad du gzugs kyi 'du shes rnams las yang dag par 'das te/ thogs
4b3(mngon pa): pa'i 'du shes rnams nub par gyur cig sna tshogs kyi 'du shes rnams yid la mi byed pas nam mkha' mtha' yas so snyam nas nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched rdzogs par byas te gnas pa dag yod de/ 'di lta ste/ nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched du skyes pa'i lha rnams so/ /
4b4(mngon pa): 'di ni sems can gyi gnas drug pa'o/ /sems can gzugs med pa rnam pa thams cad du nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched las yang dag par 'das te/ rnam par shes pa mtha' yas so snyam nas rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched rdzogs par byas te gnas pa dag yod de/
4b5(mngon pa): 'di lta ste/ rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched du skyes pa'i lha rnams so/ /'di ni sems can gyi gnas bdun pa'o/ /sems can gzugs med pa gang dag rnam pa thams cad du rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched las yang dag par 'das te/ ci yang med do snyam nas ci yang med
4b6(mngon pa): pa'i skye mched rdzogs par byas te gnas pa dag yod de/ 'di lta ste/ ci yang med pa'i skye mched du skyes pa'i lha rnams so/ /'di ni sems can gyi gnas brgyad pa'o/ /sems can gzugs med pa rnam pa thams cad du ci yang med pa'i skye mched las yang dag par 'das nas
4b7(mngon pa): 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched rdzogs par byas te gnas pa dag yod de/ 'di lta ste/ 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched du skyes pa'i lha rnams so/ /'di ni sems can gyi gnas dgu pa'o/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na/ mi dge ba bcu'i las
5a1(mngon pa): kyi lam dag yod de/ srog gcod pa dang / ma byin par len pa dang / 'dod pa la log par g.yem pa dang / brdzun du smra ba dang / phra ma dang / tshig rtsub po dang / tshig 'khyal pa dang / brnab sems dang / gnod sems dang / log par lta ba rnams so/ /srog
5a2(mngon pa): gcod pa shas cher kun du bsten cing bsgoms te/ lan mang du byas pas sems can dmyal ba chen po mnar med par skye bar 'gyur ro/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni tsha bar ro/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni ngu 'bod chen
5a3(mngon pa): por ro/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni ngu 'bod du'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni bsdus gzhom du'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni thig nag tu'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang / de bas
5a4(mngon pa): ches yang bas ni sems can dmyal ba chen po yang sos su skye bar 'gyur ro/ /ma byin par len pa shas cher kun tu bsten cing bsgoms te/ lan mang du byas pa dang / 'dod pa la log par g.yem pa dang / brdzun du smra ba dang / phra ma dang / tshig rtsub po dang / tshig 'khyal pa dang /
5a5(mngon pa): brnab sems dang / gnod sems dang / log par lta ba shas cher kun tu bsten cing bsgoms te/ lan mang du byas pas ni sems can dmyal ba chen po mnar med par skye bar 'gyur ro/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni rab tu tsha bar ro/ /de bas shas chung
5a6(mngon pa): ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni tsha bar ro/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni ngu 'bod chen por ro/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni ngu 'bod du'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni bsdus gzhom du'o/ /de
5a7(mngon pa): bas ches shes chung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni thig nag tu'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni sems can dmyal ba chen po yang sos su skye bar 'gyur ro/ /'jig rten gzhag pa las tshigs gnyis pa'o/ /mdo la/ mkha' lding las
5b1(mngon pa): lam bcu po dang / /myong ba dang ni bkres dang zas/ /bdud rtsi phyis char pa dang / /mu ge bde dang bcu tshan no/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na klu'i rigs bzhi stong rgya mtsho chen po na gnas so/ /nam mkha' lding gi rigs bzhi stong shing shal ma li mthon po la gnas te/
5b2(mngon pa): sgo nga las skye ba stong dang / mngal nas skye ba stong dang / drod gsher las skye ba stong dang / rdzus te skye ba stong rnams so/ /nam mkha' lding sgo nga las skye ba ni bza' ba'i phyir klu sgo nga las skye ba 'byin par byed de/ mngal nas skye ba ma yin/ drod gsher las skye ba ma yin/
5b3(mngon pa): rdzus te skye ba ma yin no/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ci ste de len na/ de nyid thal ba bzhin du byed par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro/ /nam mkha' lding mngal nas skyes pa ni bza' ba'i phyir klu sgo nga las skye ba dang / mngal nas skye ba 'byin par byed de/ drod gsher las skye ba ma yin/ /rdzus te skye
5b4(mngon pa): ba ma yin no/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ci ste de len na/ de nyid thal ba bzhin du byed par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro/ /nam mkha' lding drod gsher las skye ba ni bza' ba'i phyir klu sgo nga las skye ba dang / mngal nas skye ba dang / drod gsher las skye ba 'byin par byed de/ rdzus te skye ba ma yin no/ /
5b5(mngon pa): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ci ste de len na de nyid thal ba bzhin du byed par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro/ /nam mkha' lding rdzus te skye ba ni bza' ba'i phyir klu sgo nga las skye ba dang / mngal nas skye ba dang / drod gsher las skye ba dang / rdzus te skye ba 'byin par byed do/ /klu la klu chen po bskal par gnas shing
5b6(mngon pa): sa 'dzin pa dag yod do/ /de dag kyang gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ klu'i rgyal po dga' bo dang / nye dga' gnyis dang / klu'i rgyal po rtas rgyal dang / klu'i rgyal po btang bzung dang / klu'i rgyal po gzi can dang / klu'i rgyal po yul 'khor srung dang / klu'i rgyal po nag po chen po dang /
5b7(mngon pa): klu'i rgyal bo e le'i 'dab ma rnams te/ 'di dag gzhan yang klu chen po bskal par gnas shing sa 'dzin pa nam mkha' lding dag gis dbyung bar mi nus pa gang yin pa 'di dag ni lha dang lha ma yin gyi g.yul myong bar byed cing so sor myong bar byed de/ shes shing rab tu shes la/ kun
6a1(mngon pa): du rab tu shes so/ /ji skad du/ shin tu mthu che ba yi klu dag yod/ /ma mtha' srung zhing chu na gnas pa ste/ /de dag lha min dag dang g.yul 'gyed pas/ /'di dag brgya byin gyi ni dpung yang yin/ /stobs kyang che zhing dug che klu yin te/ /shin tu drag po
6a2(mngon pa): dgra thabs sna tshogs can/ /lha min rnams dang lhan cig g.yul 'gyed pas/ /de dag brgya byin gyi ni dpung yang yin/ /zhes kyang bya'o/ /bar gyi mdo la/ dga' bo nyer dga' rtas rgyal dang / /btang bzung dang ni gzi can dang / /yul 'khor srung dang nag po che/ /e le'i 'dab
6a3(mngon pa): ma phyi ma yin/ /stong spyi phud kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam dag yod de/ srog gcod pa spong ba dang / ma byin par len pa dang / 'dod pa la log par g.yem pa dang / brdzun du smra ba dang / phra ma dang / tshig rtsub po dang / tshig 'khyal pa spong ba dang / brnab
6a4(mngon pa): sems med pa dang / gnod sems med pa dang / yang dag par lta ba rnams so/ /srog gcod pa spong ba shas cher kun du bsten cing bsgoms te lan mang du byas pas ni gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye bar 'gyur ro/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang
6a5(mngon pa): de bas ches yang bas ni 'phrul dga' ba rnams so/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni dga' ldan pa rnams su'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni 'thab bral ba rnams su'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang / de bas ches yang
6a6(mngon pa): bas ni sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams su'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni rgyal chen bzhi pa rnams su'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni mi rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye bar 'gyur ro/ /ma byin par len pa dang / 'dod pa la
6a7(mngon pa): log par g.yem pa dang / brdzun du smra ba dang / phra ma dang / tshig rtsub po dang / tshig 'khyal pa spong ba dang / chags sems med pa dang / gnod sems med pa dang / yang dag par lta ba shas cher kun tu bsten cing bsgoms te lan mang du byas pas ni gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha
6b1(mngon pa): rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye bar 'gyur ro/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni 'phrul dga' ba rnams so/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni dga' ldan pa rnams su'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni
6b2(mngon pa): 'thab bral ba rnams su'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams su'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni rgyal chen bzhi pa rnams su'o/ /de bas ches shas chung ba dang / de bas ches yang bas ni mi rnams
6b3(mngon pa): dang skal ba mnyam par skye bar 'gyur ro/ /ji ste mi rnams dang skal ba mnyam par skye na yang srog gcod pa spong bas ni tshe ring por 'gyur ro/ /ma byin par len pa spong bas ni longs spyod chen por 'gyur ro/ /'dod pa la log par g.yem pa spong bas ni chung ma 'gran zla med par 'gyur ro/ /
6b4(mngon pa): brdzun du smra ba spong bas ni skur pa mang bar mi 'gyur ro/ /phra ma spong bas ni mdza' bo dang 'bye bar mi 'gyur ro/ /tshig rtsub po spong bas ni yid du mi 'ong ba'i sgra thos par mi 'gyur ro/ /tshig 'khyal pa spong bas ni tshig mnyan par 'gyur ro/ /chags sems med pas ni 'dod chags
6b5(mngon pa): che bar mi 'gyur ro/ /gnod sems med pas ni zhe sdang che bar mi 'gyur ro/ /yang dag pa'i lta bas ni gti mug che bar mi 'gyur ro/ /sems can dmyal bar myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas mnar med pa'i sems can dmyal ba chen po'i che'i
6b6(mngon pa): tshad bskal par len pa 'di mchog yin no/ /dud 'gro myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas sa srung gi bus sa srung gi bu nyid dang / rab tu brtan pas rab tu brtan pa nyid thob pa 'di mchog yin no/ /yi dags kyi skye gnas su skye bar 'gyur ba'i las
6b7(mngon pa): rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas rgyal po gshin rjes gshin rje'i 'jig rten gyi sems can rnams kyi rgyal srid kyi dbang phyug la dbang byed pa 'di ni mchog yin no/ /mi'i skye gnas myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas nga las nus pa
7a1(mngon pa): las nu nyid du thob pa 'di mchog yin no/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i ris myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas rgyal po chen po bzhi rnams rgyal srid kyi dbang phyug la dbang byed pa 'di mchog yin no/ /sum cu rtsa gsum myong bar
7a2(mngon pa): 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas brgya byin gyis brgya byin nyid thob pa 'di mchog yin no/ /'thab bral myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas rab 'thab bral nyid thob pa 'di mchog yin no/ /dga' ldan myong
7a3(mngon pa): bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas yongs su dga' ldan gyis yongs su dga' ldan nyid thob pa 'di mchog yin no/ /'phrul dga' myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas rab sprul nyid thob pa 'di mchog yin no/ /
7a4(mngon pa): gzhan 'phrul dbang byed myong bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams kyi nang na ni las gang gi rnam par smin pas dbang byed kyi dbang nyid thob pa 'di mchog yin no/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la bkres pa dang / skom pa yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags po rnams dang / nub kyi ba
7a5(mngon pa): lang spyod pa rnams dang / byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang / rgyal chen bzhi'i ris kyi lha rnams dang / sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams la yang yod do/ /de phan
7a6(mngon pa): chad la ni bkres pa dang skom pa med do/ /de ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la kha zas 'di lta ste/ 'bras chan dang / zan dang / phye dang / sha dang / khur ba rnams yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags po dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod la yang yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi
7a7(mngon pa): rnams ni ma rmos ma btab pa'i 'bras bu sA lu'i 'bru za'o/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i ris kyi lha rnams ni dri za'i zas dang bdud rtsi'i zas za'o/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams ba dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul
7b1(mngon pa): dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no/ /de yan chad la ni kham gyi zas med do/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi bdud rtsi ni rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po rnams so/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams ji
7b2(mngon pa): lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyang de bzhin no/ /tshangs ris pa rnams la ni med do/ /de yan chad la yang med do/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i
7b3(mngon pa): gling pa rnams la bshang ba dang gci ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags po rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang / byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams la yang yod do/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la ni med do/ /de yan chad la yang med do/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling
7b4(mngon pa): gi mi rnams la char 'bab mkhas pa dang / char 'bab mi mkhas pa yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang / rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la ni med do/ /de yan chad la yang med do/ /
7b5(mngon pa): ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la lo legs pa dang / mu ge yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags po dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang / rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la ni med do/ /de yan chad la yang med do/ /ji ltar
7b6(mngon pa): 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la 'jigs pa dang / bde ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags po rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams la ni med do/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams dang / sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab
7b7(mngon pa): bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams la yod do/ /tshangs ris pa rnams la ni med do/ /de yan chad la yang med do/ /'jig rten gzhag pa las tshigs gsum pa'o/ /mdo la/ nyo tshong
8a1(mngon pa): mdog dang khang pa dang / /gding ba dang ni gzhag gos dang / /yang ba rdul rab bsgre ba dang / /tha dad bag ma len dang bcu/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la nor ram/ 'bru'am/ gser ram dngul nyo tshong bya ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang
8a2(mngon pa): nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams dang / rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la ni med do/ /de yan chad la yang med do/ /'di snyam du/ 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la nor dang 'bru rnams kyi nyo tshong byed do/ /shar gyi lus 'phags po rnams ni
8a3(mngon pa): ras dang be'u ras rnams kyis so/ /nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams ni ba lang dang nor bu rnams kyis so zhes zer ba yang yod do/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams kyi mdog nag po dang / dkar po dang / sngo bsangs dang / mdog skya snar rnam pa bzhi yod pa bzhin du shar gyi
8a4(mngon pa): lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams kyang de bzhin no/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams ni mdog gcig pa ste dkar po'o/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi mdog ni rnam pa bzhi'o/ /sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po rnams so/ /rgyal chen
8a5(mngon pa): bzhi pa rnams kyi ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyang de bzhin no/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams kyang mdog gcig pa ste dkar po'o/ /tshangs ris
8a6(mngon pa): kyi lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams
8a7(mngon pa): dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no/ /nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched dang / rnam shes mtha' yas skye
8b1(mngon pa): mched dang / ci yang med pa'i skye mched dang / 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched la ni kha dog med do/ /'di ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams kyi khang pa ched du byas pa dang / ched du byas pa ma yin pa dang / khang bzangs dang / sa khang rnams yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa
8b2(mngon pa): rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams kyi khang pa ni ched du byas pa ma yin pa'i sa khang ngo / /rgyal chen bzhi pa rnams kyi gzhal med khang ni ched du byas pa dang ched du byas pa ma yin pa'o/ /rgyal chen bzhi pa'i lha rnams kyi 'jig rten
8b3(mngon pa): pa bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi yang de bzhin no/ /tshangs ris pa rnams kyi gzhal med khang rnams ni ched du byas pa ma yin pa'o/ /tshangs
8b4(mngon pa): ris pa rnams kyi ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa
8b5(mngon pa): rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min pa rnams kyi gzhal med khang yang ched du byas pa ma yin no/ /gzugs med pa
8b6(mngon pa): rnams la ni khang pa med pa'o/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la gding ba dang bgo ba 'di lta ste/ bal gos dang / sha na'i ras dang / gso ma'i ras dang / zar ma'i ras dang / ras gos dang / zab dar dang / ko tam pa'i ras dang / rtswa du ku la'i gos dang / a pa ra na ti
8b7(mngon pa): ka'i gos dang / ras dang / be'u ras yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams ni dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos gyon no/ /ji ltar byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams dpag bsam gyi
9a1(mngon pa): shing las byung ba'i gos gyon pa bzhin du rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams dang / sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no/ /tshangs
9a2(mngon pa): ris kyi lha rnams ni gos gyon bzhin du skye'o/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad
9a3(mngon pa): med dge rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams kyang de
9a4(mngon pa): gos gyon bzhin du skye'o/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams kyi dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos kyang rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po rnams so/ /gzhan gos kyang rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po
9a5(mngon pa): rnams so/ /dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos kyang rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po rnams te/ dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos ji lta bu 'dod pa de lta bu skyes pa'am/ bud med dag gis sems bskyed ma thag tu de la yal ga 'dud
9a6(mngon pa): par byed do/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos kyi shing rnams kyang rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po rnams dang / gzhan gos kyang rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar
9a7(mngon pa): po rnams so/ /dpag bsam gyi shing las byung ba'i gos kyang rnam pa bzhi ste/ sngon po dang / ser po dang / dmar po dang / dkar po rnams te/ dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos ji lta bu 'dod pa de lta bu lha'i bu'am/ lha'i bu mo dag gis sems bskyed ma thag tu yal ga 'dud
9b1(mngon pa): par byed do/ /de'i lag tu 'ong bar 'gyur ro/ /rgyal chen bzhi pa rnams kyi ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan ba rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi yang de bzhin no/ /tshangs ris kyi lha
9b2(mngon pa): rnams la ni dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos med do/ /de yan chad la yang med do/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la gding ba dang / bgo ba lci ba dang / yang ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags po rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/ /byang
9b3(mngon pa): gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams kyi dpag bsam gyi shing las byung ba'i gos la ni srang gcig yod do/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi ni srang phyed do/ /sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi ni srang gi bzhi cha gcig go/ /'thab bral ba rnams kyi ni srang gang gi brgyad cha gcig go/ /dga' ldan pa rnams
9b4(mngon pa): kyi ni srang gi bcu drug cha gcig go/ /'phrul dga' ba rnams kyi ni sum cu rtsa gnyis kyi srang gi cha gcig go / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi dpag bsam gyi shing las byung ba'i gos ni srang gi drug cu rtsa bzhi'i cha gcig las med do/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams kyi ni gzhal du med
9b5(mngon pa): pa'i gos yin no/ /tshangs ris pa rnams kyi ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas
9b6(mngon pa): pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams kyi yang gzhal du med pa'i gos yin no/ /nyi zer gyi
9b7(mngon pa): rdul bzhi bcu rtsa dgu'i cha gcig ni rdul phra rab yin no/ /rdul phra rab bdun ni rdul phra mo gcig go/ /rdul phra mo bdun la ni nyi zer gyi rdul gcig go/ /nyi zer gyi rdul bdun la ni ri bong gi rdul gcig go/ /ri bong gi rdul bdun la ni lug rdul gcig go/ /lug rdul bdun la ni glang rdul
10a1(mngon pa): gcig go/ /glang rdul bdun la ni sro ma gcig go/ /sro ma bdun la ni a ba ga na gcig go/ /a ba ga na bdun la ni ba ti ka gcig go/ /ba ti ka bdun la ni nas 'bru gcig go/ /nas 'bru bdun la ni sor gcig go/ /sor nyi shu rtsa bzhi la ni khru gang ngo / /'dzam bu'i
10a2(mngon pa): gling gi mi rnams kha cig ni khru tshad de ltar brtsis pa'i khru phyed dang bzhi pa'o/ /kha cig ni khru bzhi pa'o/ /shar gyi lus 'phags po rnams ni khru brgyad pa'o/ /nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams ni khru bcu drug pa'o/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams ni khru sum cu rtsa gnyis pa'o/ /rgyal chen
10a3(mngon pa): bzhi'i lha rnams kyi lus thob pa ni rgyang grags kyi bzhi cha gcig go/ /sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams kyi ni rgyang grags kyi phyed do/ /'thab bral ba rnams kyi ni rgyang grags kyi bzhi cha gsum pa'o/ /dga' ldan pa rnams kyi ni rgyang grags gcig go/ /'phrul dga' ba rnams kyi ni
10a4(mngon pa): rgyang grags gcig dang / rgyang grags kyi bzhi cha gcig go/ /gzhan 'phrul dbang byed rnams kyi ni rgyang grags phyed dang gnyis so/ /tshangs ris pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad phyed do/ /tshangs pa mdun na 'don pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad gcig go/ /tshangs pa chen po pa rnams kyi ni
10a5(mngon pa): dpag tshad phyed dang gnyis so/ /'od chung ba rnams kyi ni dpag tshad gnyis so/ /tshad med 'od pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad bzhi'o/ /'od gsal ba rnams kyi ni dpag tshad brgyad do/ /dge chung ba rnams kyi ni dpag tshad bcu drug go/ /tshad med dge ba rnams kyi ni dpag tshad sum cu rtsa
10a6(mngon pa): gnyis so/ /dge rgyas pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad drug cu rtsa bzhi'o/ /sprin med pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad brgya nyi shu rtsa bzhi'o/ /bsod nams skyes pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad nyis brgya lnga bcu'o/ /'bras bu che ba'i lha rnams kyi ni dpag tshad lnga brgya'o/ /'du shes med pa'i
10a7(mngon pa): sems can rnams kyi yang de dang 'dra'o/ /mi che ba'i lus thob pa ni dpag tshad stong ngo / /mi gdung ba rnams kyi ni dpag tshad nyis stong ngo / /gya nom snang ba rnams kyi ni dpag tshad bzhi stong ngo / /shin tu mthong ba pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad brgyad stong ngo / /'og min gyi lha rnams
10b1(mngon pa): kyi lus thob pa rnams kyi ni dpag tshad khri drug stong ngo / /gzugs med pa rnams la ni bsags pa'i lus med do/ /nyi zer gyi rdul bzhi bcu rtsa dgu'i cha gcig gi ni rdul phra rab yin no/ /rdul phra rab bdun la ni rdul phra mo gcig go/ /rdul phra mo bdun la ni nyi zer gyi rdul gcig
10b2(mngon pa): go/ /nyi zer gyi rdul bdun la ni ri bong gi rdul gcig go/ /ri bong gi rdul bdun la ni lug rdul gcig go/ /lug rdul bdun la ni glang rdul gcig go/ /glang rdul bdun la ni sro ma gcig go/ /sro ma bdun la ni a ba ga na gcig go/ /a ba ga na bdun la ni ba ti ka gcig go/ /
10b3(mngon pa): ba ti ka bdun la ni nas 'bru gcig go/ /nas 'bru bdun la ni sor gcig go/ /sor nyi shu rtsa bzhi la khru gang ngo / /'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams kha cig gos khru tshad 'di lta bur brtsis pa'i khru brgyad pa gyon no/ /kha cig ni khru bcu pa'o/ /shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams kyi ni khru nyi
10b4(mngon pa): shu pa'o/ /nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams kyi ni khru bzhi bcu pa'o/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams kyi ni dpag bsam shing las byung ba'i gos khru brgyad cu pa gyon no/ /rgyal chen bzhi pa'i lha rnams kyang lus la ci ran pa'i gos gyon no/ /rgyal chen bzhi pa lha rnams kyi ji lta ba bzhin du sum
10b5(mngon pa): cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams dang / tshangs ris pa rnams dang / tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams
10b6(mngon pa): dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams
10b7(mngon pa): dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min pa rnams kyi yang de bzhin no/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams dbang po tha dad do/ /kha cig la ni mo'i dbang po dang / kha cig la ni pho'i dbang po yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi
11a1(mngon pa): ba lang spyod pa rnams dang / byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang / rgyal chen bzhi pa'i lha rnams dang / sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams la yang
11a2(mngon pa): yang yod do/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni mo'i dbang po yang med/ pho'i dbang po yang med do/ /tshangs ris pa rnams ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba
11a3(mngon pa): rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba
11a4(mngon pa): rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la bag ma gtong ba dang / bag ma len pa yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams la ni med do/ /rgyal
11a5(mngon pa): chen bzhi pa'i lha rnams dang / sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams la yang yod do/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni bag ma gtong ba yang med len pa yang med do/ /
11a6(mngon pa): tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang /
11a7(mngon pa): sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams la yang de bzhin no/ /'jig rten gzhag pa las tshig
11b1(mngon pa): bzhi pa'o/ / //'jig rten gzhag pa/ bam po gnyis pa/ mdo la/ grang dang tsha dang dus tshigs mtshan mo dang / /pha ma dang ni rje khol dang / /nor dang 'bru dang mngon par zhe na/ /bcu tshan yongs su brjod pa yin/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la shin tu grang ba
11b2(mngon pa): dang / shin tu tsha ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams la ni med do/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la yang med do/ /de yan chad la yang med do/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la
11b3(mngon pa): dus tshigs 'di lta ste/ dgun dang dpyid dang dbyar yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang / byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang / rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams dang / sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga'
11b4(mngon pa): ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams la yang yod do/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni dus tshigs med do/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po rnams dang / 'od
11b5(mngon pa): chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba
11b6(mngon pa): rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams la yang de bzhin no/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la mtshan mo dang / nyin mo yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang / byang gi sgra
11b7(mngon pa): mi snyan pa rnams dang / rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams dang / sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams la yang yod do/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni mtshan mo yang med/
12a1(mngon pa): nyin mo yang med/ tshangs ris pa rnams ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang /
12a2(mngon pa): dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams la yang de bzhin no/ /ji lta ba
12a3(mngon pa): 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la pha dang ma yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang / byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang / rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams dang / sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa
12a4(mngon pa): rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams la yang yod do/ /tshangs ris pa lha rnams la ni ma yang med pha yang med do/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od
12a5(mngon pa): chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung
12a6(mngon pa): ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams la yang de bzhin no/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la rje bo dang bra na yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan
12a7(mngon pa): pa rnams la ni rje bo yang med bran kyang med do/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la ni rje bo dang bran kyang yod do/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan
12b1(mngon pa): 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams la yang de bzhin no/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni rje bo yang med bran yang med do/ /tshangs ris pa rnams la ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams
12b2(mngon pa): dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba
12b3(mngon pa): rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams la yang de bzhin no/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la nor dang 'bru yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams la yang yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams
12b4(mngon pa): la ni 'bru ni yod/ nor ni med do/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la nor ni yod 'bru ni med do/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul
12b5(mngon pa): dbang byed pa rnams la yang de bzhin no/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni nor yang med 'bru yang med do/ /tshangs ris kyi lha ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od
12b6(mngon pa): gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang /
12b7(mngon pa): shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams la yang de bzhin no/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la pha'am ma'am/ bu pho'am bu mo 'am/ rje bo'am/ bran nam/ nor ram/ 'bru la mngon par zhen pa yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi
13a1(mngon pa): ba lang spyod pa rnams la yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams la ni ci la yang mngon par zhen pa med do/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la ni 'bru ma gtogs pa rnams la mngon par zhen pa yod do/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du sum cu rtsa
13a2(mngon pa): gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi yang de bzhin no/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la yang mngon par zhen pa med do/ /tshangs ris pa rnams ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i
13a3(mngon pa): mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams
13a4(mngon pa): dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no/ /'jig rten gzhag pa las tshigs lnga pa'o/ /mdo la/ zla mtshan 'khrig dang khu chu dang / /tshig
13a5(mngon pa): bsgyur dang ni chu klung brag / sa la rdzing bu glang po dang / /srung ma 'khor los sgyur ba'i lam/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la bud med zla mtshan can dang / sbrum ma dang / bu btsa' ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang /
13a6(mngon pa): byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams la yang yod do/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi ni 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams kyi khye'u 'am bu mo lo lnga lon pa ji tsam pa de bzhin no/ /lha'am lha'i bu mo phrag pa'am phang par sems can rdzus te skye bar 'gyur te/ de la lha 'am lha'i bu mo dag 'di snyam du 'di ni
13a7(mngon pa): bdag gi bu'am bu mo snyam du sems so/ /khye'u 'am bu mo de dag kyang 'di snyam du 'di ni bdag cag gi ma'am pha'o snyam du sems so/ /sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang ni lo drug lon pa ji tsam pa bzhin no/ /'thab bral ba rnams kyi ni lo bdun lon pa ji tsam pa bzhin no/ /dga' ldan
13b1(mngon pa): ldan bye pa rnams kyi ni lo brgyad lon pa ji tsam pa bzhin no/ /'phrul dga' ba rnams kyi ni lo dgu lon pa ji tsam pa bzhin no/ /gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi ni 'dzam bu'i gling gi bu pho dang bu mo lo bcu lon pa ji tsam pa de bzhin du lha'am lha'i bu mo'i phrag pa 'am phang par rdzus te/
13b2(mngon pa): skye ba'i sems can 'byung bar 'gyur te/ de na lha'am lha'i bu mo dag 'di snyam du 'di ni bdag gi bu'am bu mo snyam du sems so/ /khye'u dang bu mo dag kyang 'di snyam du 'di ni bdag cag gi ma'am pha'o snyam du sems so/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams ni thog ma nas lus kyi yan
13b3(mngon pa): lag dang nying lag thams cad rdzogs par skye shing 'chi ba na yang de kho na nyid do/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba
13b4(mngon pa): rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu
13b5(mngon pa): mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min pa rnams kyang de bzhin no/ /gzugs med pa rnams la lus kyi gzugs med do/ /de bas na de dag gi skye ba yang mi mngon/ 'chi ba yang mi mngon no/ /ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams mi tshangs par spyod pa 'khrig pa'i chos bsten pa ni
13b6(mngon pa): gnyis kyis gnyis sbyor ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang / byang gi sgra mi snyan pa rnams dang / rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams dang / sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang de bzhin no/ /'thab bral ba rnams ni 'khyud pa tsam gyis
13b7(mngon pa): gdung ba zhi bar 'gyur ro/ /dga' ldan pa rnams kyi ni lag pa nas bzung ba tsam gyis so/ /'phrul dga' ba rnams kyi ni bgad pa tsam gyis so/ /gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi ni bltas pa tsam gyis gdung ba zhi bar 'gyur ro/ /tshangs ris pa rnams la ni 'dod chags
14a1(mngon pa): med do/ /tshangs ris pa rnams ji lta ba bzhin du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams
14a2(mngon pa): dang / dge rgyas par nams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang / bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no/ /
14a3(mngon pa): ji ltar 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la khu chu mi gtsang ba yod pa bzhin du shar gyi lus 'phags pa rnams dang / nub kyi ba lang spyod pa rnams dang / byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams la yang de bzhin no/ /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams la rlung 'byung ngo / /rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams ji lta ba
14a4(mngon pa): bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams dang / 'thab bral ba rnams dang / dga' ldan pa rnams dang / 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams kyi yang de bzhin no/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams la ni 'dod chags med do/ /tshangs ris pa rnams ji lta ba bzhin
14a5(mngon pa): du tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po pa rnams dang / 'od chung ba rnams dang / tshad med 'od pa rnams dang / 'od gsal ba rnams dang / dge chung ba rnams dang / tshad med dge ba rnams dang / dge rgyas pa rnams dang / sprin med pa rnams dang /
14a6(mngon pa): bsod nams skyes pa rnams dang / 'bras bu che ba rnams dang / mi che ba rnams dang / mi gdung ba rnams dang / gya nom snang ba rnams dang / shin tu mthong ba rnams dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams kyang de bzhin no/ /sems can dmyal ba'i sems can gyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha'
14a7(mngon pa): ni bskal pa gcig ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /dud 'gro'i skye gnas su skyes pa'i sems can rnams kyi tshe'i tshad ni mtha'i bskal pa gcig ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /mi rnams kyi nyin zhag sum cu gang yin pa de ni yi dags rnams kyi nyin gcig ste/ nyin zhag
14b1(mngon pa): de sum cu la zla ba gcig / zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ yi dags rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lo lnga brgya ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo khri lnga stong yod do/ /shar gyi lus 'phags kyi mi rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi
14b2(mngon pa): mtha' ni lo nyis brgya lnga bcu ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /nub kyi ba lang spyod kyi mi rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo lnga brgya ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba med do/ /ci'i phyir
14b3(mngon pa): byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams ni bar ma dor 'chi ba med ce na/ /de dag la bdag gi med cing yongs su 'dzin pa med de/ tshe nges shing khyad par du 'gro ba yin pas de'i phyir byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi mi rnams la bar mdor 'chi ba med do/ /'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams la ni yar skye ba dang / mar
14b4(mngon pa): 'gro ba yod de/ 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams res 'ga' ni tshe dpag tu med par 'gyur la/ res 'ga' ni tshe lo bcu par 'gyur la/ mi rnams kyi tshe lo lnga bcu gang yin pa de ni/ rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi nyin zhag gcig go/ /nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig go/ /
14b5(mngon pa): zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ rgyal chen bzhi'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lha'i lo lnga brgya ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo sa ya phrag dgu yod do/ /de ni sems can dmyal ba chen po yang sos kyi nyin zhag gcig
14b6(mngon pa): go/ /nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig /zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ sems can dmyal ba yang sos kyi sems can rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni de lo lta bur brtsis pa'i sems can dmyal ba pa'i lo lnga brgya ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de mi'i ltar
14b7(mngon pa): brtsis na lo bye ba phrag 'bum drug khri nyis stong yod do/ /mi rnams kyi lo brgya gang yin pa de ni sum cu rtsa gsum gyi nyin zhag gcig go/ /nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig /zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ sum cu rtsa gsum gyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni de lta bur brtsis
15a1(mngon pa): pa'i lha'i lo stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag gsum dang sa ya phrag drug yod do/ /de ni sems can dmyal ba chen po thig nag gi nyin zhag gcig go/ /nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig go/ /zla ba bcu
15a2(mngon pa): gnyis la lo gcig ste/ sems can dmyal ba chen po thig nag gi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i sems can dmyal ba'i lo stong ste/ bar mdor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag 'bum phrag bcu gnyis dang / bye ba phrag dgu khri drug
15a3(mngon pa): stong yod do/ /mi rnams kyi lo nyis brgya gang yin pa de ni 'thab bral gyi lha rnams kyi nyin zhag gcig go/ /nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig /zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ 'thab bral ba'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lha'i lo nyis stong ste/
15a4(mngon pa): bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag bcu bzhi dang sa ya phrag bzhi yod do/ /de ni sems can dmyal ba chen po bsdus gzhom gyi nyin zhag gcig go/ /nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig /zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ sems can dmyal ba
15a5(mngon pa): chen po bsdus gzhom gyi sems can rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i sems can dmyal ba'i lo nyis stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag gcig dang / bye ba phrag gsum 'bum drug khri brgyad stong yod do/ /mi rnams kyi lo bzhi
15a6(mngon pa): brgya gang yin pa de ni dga' ldan gyi lha rnams kyi nyin zhag gcig go/ /nyin zhag sum cu la zla ba gcig /zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ dga' ldan gyi lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lo bzhi stong yod do/ /bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de mi'i ltar
15a7(mngon pa): brtsis na lo bye ba lnga bcu rtsa bdun dang / lo sa ya phrag drug yod do/ /de ni sems can dmyal ba chen po ngu 'bod kyi nyin zhag gcig go/ /nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig /zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ sems can dmyal ba chen po ngu 'bod kyi sems can rnams kyi tshe'i
15b1(mngon pa): tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lo bzhi stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag bye ba brgya dang / bye ba phrag sa ya gnyis dang / bye ba phrag dgu 'bum bzhi khri bzhi stong yod do/ /mi rnams kyi lo brgyad brgya gang yin pa de ni 'phrul dga' lha
15b2(mngon pa): rnams kyi nyin zhag gcig go/ /nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig go/ /zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ 'phrul dga'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lha'i lo brgyad stong ste/ bar mdo'i 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag nyis
15b3(mngon pa): brgya sum cu dang / lo sa ya phrag bzhi yod do/ /de ni sems can dmyal ba chen po ngu 'bod chen po'i nyin zhag gcig go/ /nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig /zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ sems can dmyal ba chen po ngu 'bod chen po'i tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta
15b4(mngon pa): bur brtsis pa'i sems can dmyal ba'i lo brgyad stong yod de/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag drug cu rtsa drug dang / bye ba phrag sa ya gsum dang bye ba phrag lnga 'bum lnga khri nyis stong yod do/ /mi rnams kyi lo stong drug brgya gang yin pa de ni gzhan
15b5(mngon pa): 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams kyi nyin zhag gcig go/ /nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig /zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i lha'i lo khri drug stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de mi'i
15b6(mngon pa): ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag dgu brgya nyi shu rtsa gcig dang / lo sa ya drug yod de/ de ni sems can dmyal ba chen po tsha ba'i nyin zhag gcig go/ /nyin zhag de sum cu la zla ba gcig /zla ba bcu gnyis la lo gcig ste/ sems can dmyal ba chen po tsha ba'i sems can dmyal ba
15b7(mngon pa): pa'i sems can rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni lo de lta bur brtsis pa'i sems can dmyal ba pa'i lo khri drug stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /de mi'i ltar brtsis na lo bye ba phrag lnga brgya dang / lo bye ba phrag bye ba sum cu dang / lo bye ba phrag sa ya brgyad dang / bzhi 'bum dang / lo bye ba
16a1(mngon pa): phrag khri drug stong yod do/ /bar gyi mdo la/ dgu dang gsum dang bcu bzhi dang ni lnga bcu rtsa bdun dang / /nyis brgya dgu brgya rnams ni mi yi grangs kyi lha tsher bshad/ /de bzhin gcig dang bcu gnyis gcig dang brgyad dang drug cu dang / /lnga brgya dag ni sems can
16a2(mngon pa): dmyal ba pa yi tsher bshad do/ /tshangs ris kyi lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa phyed de/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /sems can dmyal ba chen po rab tu tsha ba'i che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa phyed de/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /tshangs pa'i mdun na 'don pa'i lha
16a3(mngon pa): rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa gcig yin te/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /sems can dmyal ba chen po mnar med pa'i che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa gcig ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /tshangs pa chen po pa'i lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa phyed dang
16a4(mngon pa): gnyis te/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /'od chung gi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa gnyis te/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /tshad med 'od kyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa bzhi ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /'od gsal gyi lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi
16a5(mngon pa): mtha' ni bskal pa brgyad de/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /dge chung gi lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa bcu drug ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /tshad med dge ba'i lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa sum cu rtsa gnyis te/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /
16a6(mngon pa): dge rgyas kyi lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa drug cu rtsa bzhi ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /sprin med kyi lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa brgya nyi shu rtsa lnga ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /bsod nams skyes kyi lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal
16a7(mngon pa): pa nyis brgya lnga bcu ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /'bras bu che ba'i lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa lnga brgya ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /'du shes med pa'i lha rnams kyang de dang 'dra'o/ /mi che ba'i lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa stong ste/
16b1(mngon pa): bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /mi gdung ba'i lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa nyis stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /gya nom snang ba'i lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa bzhi stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /shin tu mthong ba'i lha rnams kyi
16b2(mngon pa): tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa brgyad stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /'og min gyi lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa khri drug stong ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched pa'i che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa nyi khri ste/ bar
16b3(mngon pa): ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched pa'i lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa bzhi khri ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /ci yang med pa'i skye mched kyi lha rnams kyi che'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa drug khri ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /'du
16b4(mngon pa): shes med 'du shes med min skye mched pa'i lha rnams kyi tshe'i tshad kyi mtha' ni bskal pa brgyad khri ste/ bar ma dor 'chi ba ni yod do/ /'di nas byang phyogs na ri nag po gsum yod do/ /ri nag po gsum po de dag gi byang phyogs na ri nag po gsum yod do/ /ri nag po gzhan gsum po
16b5(mngon pa): de dag gi byang phyogs na yang ri nag po gzhan gsum yod do/ /ri nag po gzhan gsum po de dag gi byang phyogs na ri'i rgyal po gangs zhes bya ba yod do/ /ri'i rgyal po gangs kyi byang phyogs na/ ri'i rgyal po spos kyi ngad ldang zhes bya ba yod do/ /ri'i rgyal po spos kyi ngad ldang nas
16b6(mngon pa): dpag tshad bcu'i tshu rol na mtsho chen po chu zhes bya ba zhig yod de/ ma dros pa zhes kyang bya'o/ /mtsho chen po chu zhes bya ba de la chur dpag tshad lnga bcu zheng du dpag tshad lnga bcu yod do/ /mtha' skor du ni dpag tshad nyis brgya yod do/ /dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la mdzes
16b7(mngon pa): pa chu bsal zhing chu sbrang rtsi lta bus gang la/ me tog ut+pa la dang / pad+ma dang / ku mu ta dang / pad+ma dkar pos kun du khebs par 'dug go/ /de'i nang nas chu klung chen po bzhi 'di lta ste/ gang+gA dang / sin+d+hu dang / si ta dang / pak+Shu dang / 'di rnams 'bab ste/ gang+gA ni shar
17a1(mngon pa): phyogs nas glang po che'i kha nas 'bab ste/ mtsho chen po chu zhes bya ba'i g.yas phyogs su bskor nas/ klung lnga brgya dang lhan cig tu shar phyogs [(]gyi [,]kyi [)]rgya mtsho chen por 'gro'o/ /sin+d+hu ni lho phyogs nas khyu mchog gi kha nas 'bab ste/ de ni mtsho chen po chu zhes bya ba'i g.yas
17a2(mngon pa): phyogs su bskor nas klung lnga brgya dang lhan cig tu lho phyogs kyi rgya mtsho chen por 'gro'o/ /pak+Shu ni nub phyogs nas rta'i kha nas 'bab ste/ de ni mtsho chen po chu zhes bya ba'i g.yas phyogs su bskor nas/ klung lnga brgya dang lhan cig tu nub phyogs kyi rgya mtsho chen por 'gro'o/ /si ta ni byang
17a3(mngon pa): phyogs nas seng ge'i kha nas 'bab ste/ de ni mtsho chen po chu zhes bya ba'i g.yas phyogs su bskor nas/ klung lnga brgya dang lhan cig tu byang phyogs kyi rgya mtsho chen por 'gro'o/ /'di skad du/ byang phyogs kha dgur 'gyur ba yi/ /chu mtsho yod de gzhan dag kyang / /de ni mtsho chen chu
17a4(mngon pa): zhes bya/ /tha dad rgyu rnams 'byung gnas yod/ /chu klung gang+gA sin+d+hu pak+Shu dang / /si ta dba' rlabs lbu ba'i phreng ba can/ /'bab cing thams cad gsal ba'i chu yin te/ /phyogs bzhi kho ra khor yug dag nas 'byung / /gang+gA shar phyogs rgya mtshor 'gro ba ste/ /sin+d+hu lho phyogs rgya
17a5(mngon pa): mtshor 'gro ba yin/ /pak+Shu yang ni nub phyogs rgya mtshor 'gro/ /de yi byang phyogs rgya mtshor si ta 'gro/ /chu klung rab mchog bzhi po 'di dag ni/ /mchog tu bzang zhing so sor 'bab pa ste/ /re re zhing yang lnga brgya khyer nas ni/ /chu yi rgyun rnams rgya mtsho chen por 'gro/ /zhes kyang bya'o/ /
17a6(mngon pa): ri spos kyi ngad ldang de'i byang phyogs dpag tshad nyi shu na gser gyi brag bya skyibs lha ma yin gyi ngos zhes bya ba yod de/ chur dpag tshad lnga bcu zhing du yang dpag tshad lnga bcu/ mtha' skor du dpag tshad nyis brgya 'phang du dpag tshad phyed dang bzhi yod pa/ dbyibs legs shing blta na
17a7(mngon pa): sdug la mdzes pa zhig yod do/ /de'i nang gis gzhi yang dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la/ mdzes pa gser gyi bye ma bdal zhing tsan+dan gyi chus chag chag btab pa ste/ der yid du mi 'ong ba shing ngam/ /gseg ma 'am/ gang ci yang rung ba dag lhung na de mi ma yin pa
17b1(mngon pa): rnams kyi rlung gi mthus phyi rol du gtor ro/ /de'i kho ra khor yug na gser gyi brag bya skyibs can brgya stong yod do/ /de dag thams cad kyang dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la mdzes pa ste/ de dag gi nang nas gzhi rnams kyang dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la/ mdzes
17b2(mngon pa): pa gser gyi phye ma bdal zhing tsan+dan gyi chus chag chag btab pa/ de dag tu yang yid du mi 'ong ba shing ngam/ gseg ma 'am/ gang ci yang rung ba dag lhung na/ de mi ma yin pa rnams kyi rlung gi mthus phyi rol du 'dor ro/ /de'i lam srid du dpag tshad nyi shu/ zheng du dpag
17b3(mngon pa): tshad phyed dang gnyis yod pa dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la mdzes pa gser gyi phye ma bdal zhing tsan+dan gyi chus chag chag btab pa zhig yod de/ de yang yid du mi 'ong ba shing ngam gseg ma'am/ gang ci yang rung ba dag lhung na de mi ma yin pa rnams kyi rlung gi mthus phyi rol
17b4(mngon pa): du 'dor ro/ /brag bya skyibs lha ma yin gyi ngos de'i byang phyogs dpag tshad nyi shu na shing sA la'i rgyal po chen po rab tu brtan pa zhes bya ba sA la'i phreng ba rim pa bdun gyis bskor ba zhig yod do/ /sA la'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa de'i rtsa ba ni 'dom bcu bzhi thur du zug go/ /sA la'i
17b5(mngon pa): phreng ba dang po'i rtsa ba ni 'dom bcu gsum thur du zug go/ /gnyis pa'i ni bcu gnyis so/ /gsum pa'i ni bcu gcig go/ /bzhi pa'i ni bcu'o/ /lnga pa'i ni dgu'o/ /drug pa'i ni brgyad do/ /sA la'i phreng ba bdun pa'i rtsa ba ni 'dom bdun thur du zug go/ /sA la'i rgyal po rab
17b6(mngon pa): tu brtan pa de'i yal ga dang / lo ma dang yal ga rnams gang yin pa de ni sA la'i phreng ba dang po la thug go/ /sA la'i phreng ba dang po ni yal ga dang lo ma dang yal ga gang yin pa de ni gnyis pa la'o/ /gnyis pa'i gang yin pa de ni gsum pa la'o/ /gsum pa'i gang yin pa de ni bzhi
17b7(mngon pa): pa la'o/ /bzhi pa'i gang yin pa de ni lnga pa la'o/ /lnga pa'i gang yin pa de ni drug pa la'o/ /drug pa'i gang yin pa de ni bdun pa la'o/ /sA la'i phreng ba bdun pa'i yal ga dang / lo ma dang yal ga gang yin pa de ni nam mkha' khyab par 'dug go/ /de'i nang gi sa gzhi yang
18a1(mngon pa): dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la/ mdzes pa gser gyi phye ma bdal zhing tsan+dan gyi chus chag chag btab pa ste/ de yang yid du mi 'ong ba shing ngam gseg ma'am/ gang ci yang rung ba dag lhung na ni de mi ma yin pa rnams kyi rlung gi mthus phyi rol tu 'dor
18a2(mngon pa): ro/ /de'i lam srid du dpag tshad nyi shu/ zheng du dpag tshad phyed dang gnyis yod pa/ dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la mdzes pa zhig yod do/ /der yang yid du mi 'ong ba shing ngam gseg ma'am gang ci yang rung ba dag lhung na de mi ma yin pa rnams kyi rlung gi mthus phyi rol
18a3(mngon pa): du 'dor ro/ /sA la'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa'i shar phyogs dpag tshad nyi shu na/ rdzing bu dal gyis 'bab ces bya ba chur dpag tshad lnga bcu/ zheng du yang dpag tshad lnga bcu ste/ mtha' skor du dpag tshad nyis brgya yod pa/ dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la mdzes pa chu
18a4(mngon pa): bsil zhing chu sbrang rtsi lta bus gang ba/ me tog ut+pa la dang / pad+ma dang / ku mu ta dang / pad+ma dkar pos khebs pa zhig yod do/ /rdzing bu dal gyis 'bab pa de'i nang gi pad+ma'i lo ma rnams che zhing mchog tu che ste/ 'di lta ste/ ba lang gi ko ba tsam mo/ /pad+ma'i sdong bu rnams che zhing mchog
18a5(mngon pa): tu che ste/ 'di lta ste/ gshol mda' tsam mo/ /pad+ma'i me tog rnams che zhing mchog tu che ste/ 'di lta ste/ shing rta'i 'phang lo tsam mo/ /pad+ma'i rtsa ba rnams che zhing mchog tu che ste/ 'di lta ste/ skyes bu chen po'i brla tsam mo/ /ro mngar zhing mchog tu mngar ste/ 'di lta ste/ sbrang
18a6(mngon pa): bu'i sbrang rtsi ma bskol ba bzhin no/ /bcad na yang 'o ma 'dzag go/ /rdzing bu dal gyis 'bab kyi kho ra khor yug na rdzing bu brgyad stong yod de/ de dag thams cad kyang dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la mdzes pa chu bsil zhing sbrang rtsi lta bus gang ngo / /de dag gi nang gi pad+ma'i lo ma
18a7(mngon pa): rnams kyang che zhing mchog tu che ste/ 'di lta ste/ ba lang gi ko ba tsam mo/ /pad+ma'i sdong bu rnams che zhing mchog tu che ste/ 'di lta ste/ gshol mda' tsam mo/ /pad+ma'i me tog rnams che zhing mchog tu che ste/ 'di lta ste/ shing rta'i 'phang lo tsam mo/ /pad+ma'i rtsa ba rnams che zhing
18b1(mngon pa): mchog tu che ste/ 'di lta ste/ skyes bu chen po'i brla tsam mo/ /ro mngar zhing mchog tu mngar te/ 'di lta ste/ sbrang bu'i sbrang rtsi ma bskol ba bzhin no/ /bcad na yang 'o ma 'dzag go/ /de'i lam srid du dpag tshad nyi shu/ zhing du dpag tshad phyed dang gnyis yod pa/
18b2(mngon pa): dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la mdzes pa gser gyi phye ma bdal zhing tsan+dan gyi chus chag chag btab pa zhig yod de/ der yang yid du mi 'ong ba shing ngam/ gseg ma'am/ gang ci yang rung bdag lhung na de mi ma yin pa rnams kyi rlung gi mthus phyi rol du 'dor ro/ /
18b3(mngon pa): sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi glang po che'i rgyal po g.yul dor chas pa rab tu brtan pa zhes bya ba gzugs bzang zhing blta na sdug la mdzes pa zhig yod de/ me tog ku mu ta'i mdog ltar thal kar du 'dug la/ yan lag bdun shin tu legs par gnas pa ste/
18b4(mngon pa): de mgo bo yang dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la mdzes pa ste/ sngo zhing srog chags lham bu chug sher gyi mdog ltar dbus dmar la mche ba drug yod de/ glang po che rab tu brtan pa srid du dpag tshad phyed dang gsum/ zheng du dpag tshad gcig 'phang du dpag tshad phyed
18b5(mngon pa): dang gnyis/ mtha' skor du dpag tshad bdun yod do/ /de'i 'khor glang po che brgyad stong yod do/ /de thams cad kyang gzugs bzang zhing blta na sdug pa mdzes pa/ me tog ku mu ta'i mdog ltar thal kar du 'dug cing yan lag bdun shin tu legs par gnas pa ste/ de
18b6(mngon pa): dag gi mgo bo yang dbyibs legs shing blta na sdug la mdzes pa ste/ sngo zhing srog chags lham bu chu gsher gyi mdog ltar dbus dmar la mche ba drug yod pa sha stag ste/ glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa de 'khor dang bcas pa dgun zla ba bzhi ni brag bya
18b7(mngon pa): skyibs lha ma yin gyi ngos kyi nang na gnas shing 'khod do/ /dpyid zla ba bzhi ni shing sA la'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa'i nang na gnas shing 'khod do/ /dbyar zla ba bzhi ni rdzing bu dal gyis 'bab kyi nang na gnas shing 'khod do/ /gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan
19a1(mngon pa): pa brag bya skyibs lha ma yin gyi ngos kyi nang na gnas shing 'dug pa de'i tshe ni glang po che brgyad stong po rnams 'di lta ste/ glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa srung ba dang sba ba dang mdzes par bya ba'i phyir brag bya skyibs brgyad stong gi nang na nye bar gnas shing 'khod
19a2(mngon pa): do/ /gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa brag bya skyibs lha ma yin gyi ngos kyi nang na gnas shing sA la'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa'i nang du 'gro ba na/ res 'ga' ni tha mal pa'i tshul gyis 'gro'o/ /res 'ga' ni 'di lta ste/ lha dang lha'i bu rdzu 'phrul che zhing gang yang rung ba
19a3(mngon pa): dang 'dra bar bdag nyid mngon par sprul nas glang po che thams cad kyi nang na dbang che bar grags pa gang yin pa de nyid kyi mgo bo'am/ rgyab tu zhon te sil snyan dang pheg rdob pa dag cher byed cing 'gro'o/ /gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa'i nang na gnas shing 'dug pa de'i tshe ni
19a4(mngon pa): glang po che brgyad stong po 'di dag kyang 'di lta ste/ glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa srung ba dang / spa ba dang / mdzes par bya ba'i phyir shing sA la'i phreng ba rim pa bdun po dag gi nang na kha nang du bltas shing 'khod do/ /shing sA la'i phreng ba dang po'i nang na 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag
19a5(mngon pa): kyang kha nang du bltas te 'khod do/ /gnyis pa'i nang na 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag kyang kha nang du lta'o/ /gsum pa'i nang du 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag kyang kha nang du lta'o/ /bzhi pa'i nang du 'dug pa de dag kyang kha nang du lta'o/ /lnga pa'i nang na 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag kyang
19a6(mngon pa): kha nang du lta'o/ /drug pa'i nang na 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag kyang kha nang du lta'o/ /bdun pa'i nang na 'dug pa gang yin pa de dag kyang kha nang du bltas te 'khod do/ /gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa shing sA la'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa nas rdzing bu dal gyis 'bab par
19a7(mngon pa): 'gro ba na/ res 'ga' ni tha mal pa'i tshul gyis 'gro'o/ /res 'ga' ni 'di lta ste/ lha'am lha'i bu rdzu 'phrul che zhing mthu che ba gang yang rung ba dang 'dra bar bdag nyid mngon par sprul nas glang po che de dag thams cad kyi nang na dbang che bar grags pa gang yin pa de nyid kyi mgo
19b1(mngon pa): 'am/ rgyab tu zhon te sil snyan dang pheg rdob pa dag rgya cher byed cing 'gro'o/ /gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa rdzing bu dal gyis 'bab kyi nang du zhugs nas rtse zhing dga' la dga' dgur spyod pa de'i tshe glang po che brgyad stong po de dag 'di lta ste/ glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan
19b2(mngon pa): pa de srung ba dang / sba ba dang / mdzes par bya ba'i phyir rdzing bu dal gyis 'bab kyi mtha' kho ra khor yug nas bskor te kha nang du bltas shing 'khod do/ /gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa rdzing bu dal gyis 'bab kyi nang nas rtse zhing dga' la dga' mgur spyad nas phyir byung ba de'i tshe nang
19b3(mngon pa): na glang po che dbang che bar grags pa gang yin pa de rdzing bu dal gyis 'bab kyi nang du zhugs nas pad+ma'i rtsa ba rnams blangs te/ shin tu bkrus shing rab tu bshal nas glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pa la 'bul lo/ /gang gi tshe glang po che'i rgyal po rab tu brtan pas zos shing 'thungs te
19b4(mngon pa): 'grangs par gyur pa de'i tshe glang po che gzhan brgyad stong po de dag kyang rdzing bu brgyad stong gi nang na rdzing bu re re zhugs na rtse zhing dga' la dga' dgur spyod do/ /pad+ma'i rtsa ba dag blangs nas shin tu bkrus shing rab tu bshal te za'o/ /sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi glang po che rgyal po
19b5(mngon pa): g.yul ngor spyad pa rab tu bstan pa'i mthu ni de tsam mo/ /sems can thams cad ni srung ma dang bcas shing srung ba dang / skyob pa dang sbed pa dang / mi 'bral ste/ sems can gang dbang chung bar grags shing bsod nams chung la/ gzi brjid chung ba de dag ni brgya phrag mang po dang / stong phrag
19b6(mngon pa): mang po la gcig srung ste/ dper na ba lang ngam lug brgya phrag mang po dang stong phrag mang po la gcig srung ba de bzhin du/ sems can gang dbang chung bar grags shing bsod nams chung la/ gzi brjid chung ba de dag ni brgya phrag mang po dang / stong phrag mang po la gcig bsrung ngo / /
19b7(mngon pa): sems can gang dbang che bar grags shing bsod nams che la gzi brjid che ba de dag ni brgya phrag mang po dang / stong phrag mang po dag gis gcig tu bsrung ste/ dper na 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po'am/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas
20a1(mngon pa): la brgya phrag mang po dang / stong phrag mang po dag gis gcig tu srung ba de bzhin du sems can gang dbang che bar grags shing bsod nams che la gzi brjid che ba de dag la brgya phrag mang po dang / stong phrag mang po dag gis gcig tu srung ngo / /'dir smras pa/
20a2(mngon pa): ji ste sems can thams cad srung ma dang bcas shing srung ba dang / skyob pa dang / sbed pa dang mi 'bral na ci'i phyir 'tshe ba yod par 'gyur/ smras pa/ srung ma mthu chung ba zhig yin na de la zil gyis gnon pa la 'tshe ba yod do/ /srung ma bag med cing bag med par gnas pa
20a3(mngon pa): zhig yin na ni bag med pa'i rgyu las kyang 'tshe ba rnams yod do/ /srung ma gnyis lhan cig mthun par gyur pas kyang zil gyis mnan nas 'tshe bar byed do/ /mi rnams chos ma yin pa spyod cing mi rigs pa spyod pa zhig yin na de dag gis chos ma yin pa spyod pa dang / mi rigs pa
20a4(mngon pa): spyod pa las kyang 'tshe ba yod do/ / //'jig rten gzhag pa/ bam po gsum pa/ sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyi mi rnams kyi srung ma 'di lta ste/ lam po che dang / srang dang / bzhi mdo dang / sum mdo dang / dri 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang / me tog
20a5(mngon pa): phreng ba 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang / zong dgram pa'i gnas rnams dang / btung ba 'tshong ba'i gnas rnams dang / rtag tu myos pa'i gnas rnams dang / gsod byed kyi gnas su bkod pa dag yod de/ zla ba phyed kyi tshes brgyad la rgyal po chen po bzhi po dag gi g.yog zho shas

28a7(mngon pa): kyis/ /lha yi grong khyer dag na rlung chen ldang / /me tog rnying pa rnams ni 'dor bar byed/ /me tog gsar pa rnams ni legs par dgram/ /zhes kyang bya'o/ /lha'i grong khyer de ni sgo stong du gcig gis ma tshang ba yod do/ /sgo gcig gi yang 'phang du ni dpag tshad phyed dang gsum/
